HTML Template Specifications\n\n### 2.1. dashboard.html\n- File Path: templates/dashboard.html\n- Page Title: Food Delivery Dashboard\n- Layout Overview: Container div with featured restaurants and navigation buttons leading to main functionalities.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `dashboard-page` (Div)\n  - `featured-restaurants` (Div)\n  - `browse-restaurants-button` (Button)\n  - `view-cart-button` (Button)\n  - `active-orders-button` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `browse-restaurants-button`: url_for('browse_restaurants')\n  - `view-cart-button`: url_for('view_cart')\n  - `active-orders-button`: url_for('active_orders')\n\n### 2.2. restaurants.html\n- File Path: templates/restaurants.html\n- Page Title: Browse Restaurants\n- Layout Overview: Search and filter controls above a grid of restaurant cards.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `restaurants-page` (Div)\n  - `search-input` (Input)\n  - `cuisine-filter` (Dropdown)\n  - `restaurants-grid` (Div)\n  - `view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}`: url_for('restaurant_menu', restaurant_id=restaurant_id)\n- Dynamic Element ID Pattern:\n  - Buttons in restaurant cards: `view-restaurant-button-{{ restaurant_id }}`\n\n### 2.3. menu.html\n- File Path: templates/menu.html\n- Page Title: Restaurant Menu\n- Layout Overview: Restaurant info header followed by a grid of menu items.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `menu-page` (Div)\n  - `restaurant-name` (H1)\n  - `restaurant-info` (Div)\n  - `menu-items-grid` (Div)\n  - `add-to-cart-button-{item_id}` (Button)\n  - `view-item-details-{item_id}` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `add-to-cart-button-{item_id}`: (functionality to add item to cart)\n  - `view-item-details-{item_id}`: url_for('item_details', item_id=item_id)\n- Dynamic Element ID Pattern:\n  - Add to Cart Buttons: `add-to-cart-button-{{ item_id }}`\n  - View Details Buttons: `view-item-details-{{ item_id }}`\n\n### 2.4. item_details.html\n- File Path: templates/item_details.html\n- Page Title: Item Details\n- Layout Overview: Detailed view of a menu item with quantity input and add to cart button.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `item-details-page` (Div)\n  - `item-name` (H1)\n  - `item-description` (Div)\n  - `item-price` (Div)\n  - `quantity-input` (Input number)\n  - `add-to-cart-button` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `add-to-cart-button`: (adds item with quantity to cart)\n\n### 2.5. cart.html\n- File Path: templates/cart.html\n- Page Title: Shopping Cart\n- Layout Overview: Table of cart items with quantity inputs and remove buttons plus checkout button.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `cart-page` (Div)\n  - `cart-items-table` (Table)\n  - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input number)\n  - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button)\n  - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button)\n  - `total-amount` (Div)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `proceed-checkout-button`: url_for('checkout')\n- Dynamic Element ID Pattern:\n  - Quantity Inputs: `update-quantity-{{ item_id }}`\n  - Remove Buttons: `remove-item-button-{{ item_id }}`\n\n### 2.6. checkout.html\n- File Path: templates/checkout.html\n- Page Title: Checkout\n- Layout Overview: Form with fields for delivery and payment info and place order button.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `checkout-page` (Div)\n  - `customer-name` (Input)\n  - `delivery-address` (Textarea)\n  - `phone-number` (Input)\n  - `payment-method` (Dropdown)\n  - `place-order-button` (Button)\n\n### 2.7. active_orders.html\n- File Path: templates/active_orders.html\n- Page Title: Active Orders\n- Layout Overview: List of current orders with filter and buttons to track orders.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `active-orders-page` (Div)\n  - `orders-list` (Div)\n  - `track-order-button-{order_id}` (Button)\n  - `status-filter` (Dropdown)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard')\n  - `track-order-button-{order_id}`: url_for('track_order', order_id=order_id)\n- Dynamic Element ID Pattern:\n  - Track Buttons: `track-order-button-{{ order_id }}`\n\n### 2.8. track_order.html\n- File Path: templates/track_order.html\n- Page Title: Track Order\n- Layout Overview: Display detailed tracking info with back button.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `tracking-page` (Div)\n  - `order-details` (Div)\n  - `delivery-driver-info` (Div)\n  - `estimated-time` (Div)\n  - `order-items-list` (Div)\n  - `back-to-orders` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `back-to-orders`: url_for('active_orders')\n\n### 2.9. reviews.html\n- File Path: templates/reviews.html\n- Page Title: Order Reviews\n- Layout Overview: List of reviews with filtering and navigation buttons.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `reviews-page` (Div)\n  - `reviews-list` (Div)\n  - `write-review-button` (Button)\n  - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `write-review-button`: url_for('write_review')\n  - Data Schemas\n\n### 3.1. restaurants.txt\n- File name: restaurants.txt\n- Fields (order separated by | ): restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order\n- Purpose: Stores restaurant details including identification, cuisine type, location, contact, rating, delivery time, and minimum order amount.\n- Data types:\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - name: string\n  - cuisine: string\n  - address: string\n  - phone: string\n  - rating: float\n  - delivery_time: int (minutes)\n  - min_order: float\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00\n  2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00\n  3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00\n  ```\n\n### 3.2. menus.txt\n- File name: menus.txt\n- Fields: item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability\n- Purpose: Stores menu items belonging to restaurants, their categorization, descriptions, prices, and availability status.\n- Data types:\n  - item_id: int\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - item_name: string\n  - category: string\n  - description: string\n  - price: float\n  - availability: int (1 or 0)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1\n  2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1\n  3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1\n  ```\n\n### 3.3. cart.txt\n- File name: cart.txt\n- Fields: cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date\n- Purpose: Stores the current shopping cart items with quantities and added dates.\n- Data types:\n  - cart_id: int\n  - item_id: int\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - quantity: int\n  - added_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|3|2|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n### 3.4. orders.txt\n- File name: orders.txt\n- Fields: order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number\n- Purpose: Stores order records including customer info, restaurant, order date, amount, status, and delivery info.\n- Data types:\n  - order_id: int\n  - customer_name: string\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - order_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - total_amount: float\n  - status: string\n  - delivery_address: string\n  - phone_number: string\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234\n  2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678\n  ```\n\n### 3.5. order_items.txt\n- File name: order_items.txt\n- Fields: order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price\n- Purpose: Stores individual items per order, quantities, and price at order time.\n- Data types:\n  - order_item_id: int\n  - order_id: int\n  - item_id: int\n  - quantity: int\n  - price: float\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|12.99\n  2|1|2|1|8.99\n  3|2|3|1|14.99\n  ```\n\n### 3.6. deliveries.txt\n- File name: deliveries.txt\n- Fields: delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time\n- Purpose: Stores delivery details including driver information, vehicle, delivery status, and ETA.\n- Data types:\n  - delivery_id: int\n  - order_id: int\n  - driver_name: string\n  - driver_phone: string\n  - vehicle_info: string\n  - status: string\n  - estimated_time: date-time string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45\n  2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30\n  ```\n\n### 3.7. reviews.txt\n- File name: reviews.txt\n- Fields: review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date\n- Purpose: Stores customer reviews for restaurants including rating and review text.\n- Data types:\n  - review_id: int\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - customer_name: string\n  - rating: int (stars)\n  - review_text: string\n  - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12\n  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13\n  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### Notes:\n- The root `/` route redirects to `/dashboard` to comply with start page requirement.\n- The write review page element IDs are inferred as the original description lacks specific IDs and elements for that page.\n- All context and variable names adhere strictly to snake_case.\n- All element IDs use exact casing and spelling as provided.\n- Navigation IDs map exactly to route functions using Flask's `url_for()` in parentheses.\n- Templates reflect each page as specified, providing clear frontend development guidance.\n- Data schemas provide field order, types, purpose, and examples for backend data processing.\n\nThis completes the comprehensive design specification for the FoodDelivery web application.\n\n---\n\n",

`submit-review-button` (Button) <!-- For submitting review -->\n\n*(Note: The write review page elements and IDs are inferred logically since the requirements specify navigation but not page elements explicitly.)*\n\n---\n\n## 3. Data Schemas\n\n### 3.1. restaurants.txt\n- File name: restaurants.txt\n- Fields (order separated by | ): restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order\n- Purpose: Stores restaurant details including identification, cuisine type, location, contact, rating, delivery time, and minimum order amount.\n- Data types:\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - name: string\n  - cuisine: string\n  - address: string\n  - phone: string\n  - rating: float\n  - delivery_time: int (minutes)\n  - min_order: float\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00\n  2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00\n  3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00\n  ```\n\n### 3.2. menus.txt\n- File name: menus.txt\n- Fields: item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability\n- Purpose: Stores menu items belonging to restaurants, their categorization, descriptions, prices, and availability status.\n- Data types:\n  - item_id: int\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - item_name: string\n  - category: string\n  - description: string\n  - price: float\n  - availability: int (1 or 0)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1\n  2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1\n  3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1\n  ```\n\n### 3.3. cart.txt\n- File name: cart.txt\n- Fields: cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date\n- Purpose: Stores the current shopping cart items with quantities and added dates.\n- Data types:\n  - cart_id: int\n  - item_id: int\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - quantity: int\n  - added_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|3|2|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n### 3.4. orders.txt\n- File name: orders.txt\n- Fields: order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number\n- Purpose: Stores order records including customer info, restaurant, order date, amount, status, and delivery info.\n- Data types:\n  - order_id: int\n  - customer_name: string\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - order_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - total_amount: float\n  - status: string\n  - delivery_address: string\n  - phone_number: string\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234\n  2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678\n  ```\n\n### 3.5. order_items.txt\n- File name: order_items.txt\n- Fields: order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price\n- Purpose: Stores individual items per order, quantities, and price at order time.\n- Data types:\n  - order_item_id: int\n  - order_id: int\n  - item_id: int\n  - quantity: int\n  - price: float\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|12.99\n  2|1|2|1|8.99\n  3|2|3|1|14.99\n  ```\n\n### 3.6. deliveries.txt\n- File name: deliveries.txt\n- Fields: delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time\n- Purpose: Stores delivery details including driver information, vehicle, delivery status, and ETA.\n- Data types:\n  - delivery_id: int\n  - order_id: int\n  - driver_name: string\n  - driver_phone: string\n  - vehicle_info: string\n  - status: string\n  - estimated_time: date-time string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45\n  2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30\n  ```\n\n### 3.7. reviews.txt\n- File name: reviews.txt\n- Fields: review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date\n- Purpose: Stores customer reviews for restaurants including rating and review text.\n- Data types:\n  - review_id: int\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - customer_name: string\n  - rating: int (stars)\n  - review_text: string\n  - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12\n  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13\n  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### Notes:\n- The root `/` route redirects to `/dashboard` to comply with start page requirement.\n- The write review page element IDs are inferred as the original description lacks specific IDs and elements for that page.\n- All context and variable names adhere strictly to snake_case.\n- All element IDs use exact casing and spelling as provided.\n- Navigation IDs map exactly to route functions using Flask's `url_for()` in parentheses.\n- Templates reflect each page as specified, providing clear frontend development guidance.\n- Data schemas provide field order, types, purpose, and examples for backend data processing.\n\nThis completes the comprehensive design specification for the FoodDelivery web application.\n\n---\n\n",

        | POST           | N/A                   | N/A                                               | N/A                              |\n| `/checkout`                  | checkout                  | GET, POST      | checkout.html          | (GET) , (POST) order_confirmation: dict or None    | N/A                              |\n| `/orders/active`             | active_orders             | GET            | active_orders.html     | active_orders: list, status_options: list          | N/A                              |\n| `/orders/track/<int:order_id>`| track_order              | GET            | track_order.html       | order: dict, delivery_info: dict, order_items: list | order_id: int                    |\n| `/reviews`                   | reviews                   | GET            | reviews.html           | reviews: list, rating_filter_options: list         | N/A                              |\n| `/reviews/write`             | write_review              | GET, POST      | write_review.html      | (GET) , (POST) submission_status: bool or None     | N/A                              |\n\n**Explanation:**\n- Root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.\n- POST routes are for updating cart and submitting reviews.\n- Template context variables use snake_case naming matching the purpose.\n- Parameter names reflect the dynamic parts of the route.\n\n\n## 2. HTML Template Specifications\n\n### 2.1. dashboard.html\n- File Path: templates/dashboard.html\n- Page Title: Food Delivery Dashboard\n- Layout Overview: Container div with featured restaurants and navigation buttons leading to main functionalities.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `dashboard-page` (Div)\n  - `featured-restaurants` (Div)\n  - `browse-restaurants-button` (Button)\n  - `view-cart-button` (Button)\n  - `active-orders-button` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `browse-restaurants-button`: url_for('browse_restaurants')\n  - `view-cart-button`: url_for('view_cart')\n  - `active-orders-button`: url_for('active_orders')\n\n### 2.2. restaurants.html\n- File Path: templates/restaurants.html\n- Page Title: Browse Restaurants\n- Layout Overview: Search and filter controls above a grid of restaurant cards.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `restaurants-page` (Div)\n  - `search-input` (Input)\n  - `cuisine-filter` (Dropdown)\n  - `restaurants-grid` (Div)\n  - `view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}`: url_for('restaurant_menu', restaurant_id=restaurant_id)\n- Dynamic Element ID Pattern:\n  - Buttons in restaurant cards: `view-restaurant-button-{{ restaurant_id }}`\n\n### 2.3. menu.html\n- File Path: templates/menu.html\n- Page Title: Restaurant Menu\n- Layout Overview: Restaurant info header followed by a grid of menu items.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `menu-page` (Div)\n  - `restaurant-name` (H1)\n  - `restaurant-info` (Div)\n  - `menu-items-grid` (Div)\n  - `add-to-cart-button-{item_id}` (Button)\n  - `view-item-details-{item_id}` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `add-to-cart-button-{item_id}`: (functionality to add item to cart)\n  - `view-item-details-{item_id}`: url_for('item_details', item_id=item_id)\n- Dynamic Element ID Pattern:\n  - Add to Cart Buttons: `add-to-cart-button-{{ item_id }}`\n  - View Details Buttons: `view-item-details-{{ item_id }}`\n\n### 2.4. item_details.html\n- File Path: templates/item_details.html\n- Page Title: Item Details\n- Layout Overview: Detailed view of a menu item with quantity input and add to cart button.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `item-details-page` (Div)\n  - `item-name` (H1)\n  - `item-description` (Div)\n  - `item-price` (Div)\n  - `quantity-input` (Input number)\n  - `add-to-cart-button` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `add-to-cart-button`: (adds item with quantity to cart)\n\n### 2.5. cart.html\n- File Path: templates/cart.html\n- Page Title: Shopping Cart\n- Layout Overview: Table of cart items with quantity inputs and remove buttons plus checkout button.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `cart-page` (Div)\n  - `cart-items-table` (Table)\n  - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input number)\n  - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button)\n  - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button)\n  - `total-amount` (Div)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `proceed-checkout-button`: url_for('checkout')\n- Dynamic Element ID Pattern:\n  - Quantity Inputs: `update-quantity-{{ item_id }}`\n  - Remove Buttons: `remove-item-button-{{ item_id }}`\n\n### 2.6. checkout.html\n- File Path: templates/checkout.html\n- Page Title: Checkout\n- Layout Overview: Form with fields for delivery and payment info and place order button.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `checkout-page` (Div)\n  - `customer-name` (Input)\n  - `delivery-address` (Textarea)\n  - `phone-number` (Input)\n  - `payment-method` (Dropdown)\n  - `place-order-button` (Button)\n\n### 2.7. active_orders.html\n- File Path: templates/active_orders.html\n- Page Title: Active Orders\n- Layout Overview: List of current orders with filter and buttons to track orders.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `active-orders-page` (Div)\n  - `orders-list` (Div)\n  - `track-order-button-{order_id}` (Button)\n  - `status-filter` (Dropdown)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard')\n  - `track-order-button-{order_id}`: url_for('track_order', order_id=order_id)\n- Dynamic Element ID Pattern:\n  - Track Buttons: `track-order-button-{{ order_id }}`\n\n### 2.8. track_order.html\n- File Path: templates/track_order.html\n- Page Title: Track Order\n- Layout Overview: Display detailed tracking info with back button.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `tracking-page` (Div)\n  - `order-details` (Div)\n  - `delivery-driver-info` (Div)\n  - `estimated-time` (Div)\n  - `order-items-list` (Div)\n  - `back-to-orders` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `back-to-orders`: url_for('active_orders')\n\n### 2.9. reviews.html\n- File Path: templates/reviews.html\n- Page Title: Order Reviews\n- Layout Overview: List of reviews with filtering and navigation buttons.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `reviews-page` (Div)\n  - `reviews-list` (Div)\n  - `write-review-button` (Button)\n  - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `write-review-button`: url_for('write_review')\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard')\n\n### 2.10. write_review.html\n- File Path: templates/write_review.html\n- Page Title: Write Review\n- Layout Overview: Form to submit a review.\n- Element IDs:\n  - `write-review-page` (Div)  <!-- Note: not specified in requirements, logically added -->\n  - `review-form` (Form)       <!-- Logical grouping -->\n  - `restaurant-select` (Dropdown) <!-- Presumed for selecting a restaurant when writing review -->\n  - `customer-name-input` (Input)  <!-- For entering customer name -->\n  - `rating-select` (Dropdown)      <!-- For selecting rating -->\n  - `review-textarea` (Textarea)    <!-- For review text -->\n  - `submit-review-button` (Button) <!-- For submitting review -->\n\n*(Note: The write review page elements and IDs are inferred logically since the requirements specify navigation but not page elements explicitly.)*\n\n---\n\n## 3. Data Schemas\n\n### 3.1. restaurants.txt\n- File name: restaurants.txt\n- Fields (order separated by | ): restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order\n- Purpose: Stores restaurant details including identification, cuisine type, location, contact, rating, delivery time, and minimum order amount.\n- Data types:\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - name: string\n  - cuisine: string\n  - address: string\n  - phone: string\n  - rating: float\n  - delivery_time: int (minutes)\n  - min_order: float\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00\n  2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00\n  3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00\n  ```\n\n### 3.2. menus.txt\n- File name: menus.txt\n- Fields: item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability\n- Purpose: Stores menu items belonging to restaurants, their categorization, descriptions, prices, and availability status.\n- Data types:\n  - item_id: int\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - item_name: string\n  - category: string\n  - description: string\n  - price: float\n  - availability: int (1 or 0)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1\n  2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1\n  3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1\n  ```\n\n### 3.3. cart.txt\n- File name: cart.txt\n- Fields: cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date\n- Purpose: Stores the current shopping cart items with quantities and added dates.\n- Data types:\n  - cart_id: int\n  - item_id: int\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - quantity: int\n  - added_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|3|2|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n### 3.4. orders.txt\n- File name: orders.txt\n- Fields: order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number\n- Purpose: Stores order records including customer info, restaurant, order date, amount, status, and delivery info.\n- Data types:\n  - order_id: int\n  - customer_name: string\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - order_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - total_amount: float\n  - status: string\n  - delivery_address: string\n  - phone_number: string\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234\n  2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678\n  ```\n\n### 3.5. order_items.txt\n- File name: order_items.txt\n- Fields: order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price\n- Purpose: Stores individual items per order, quantities, and price at order time.\n- Data types:\n  - order_item_id: int\n  - order_id: int\n  - item_id: int\n  - quantity: int\n  - price: float\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|12.99\n  2|1|2|1|8.99\n  3|2|3|1|14.99\n  ```\n\n### 3.6. deliveries.txt\n- File name: deliveries.txt\n- Fields: delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time\n- Purpose: Stores delivery details including driver information, vehicle, delivery status, and ETA.\n- Data types:\n  - delivery_id: int\n  - order_id: int\n  - driver_name: string\n  - driver_phone: string\n  - vehicle_info: string\n  - status: string\n  - estimated_time: date-time string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45\n  2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30\n  ```\n\n### 3.7. reviews.txt\n- File name: reviews.txt\n- Fields: review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date\n- Purpose: Stores customer reviews for restaurants including rating and review text.\n- Data types:\n  - review_id: int\n  - restaurant_id: int\n  - customer_name: string\n  - rating: int (stars)\n  - review_text: string\n  - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Example rows:\n  ```\n  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12\n  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13\n  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### Notes:\n- The root `/` route redirects to `/dashboard` to comply with start page requirement.\n- The write review page element IDs are inferred as the original description lacks specific IDs and elements for that page.\n- All context and variable names adhere strictly to snake_case.\n- All element IDs use exact casing and spelling as provided.\n- Navigation IDs map exactly to route functions using Flask's `url_for()` in parentheses.\n- Templates reflect each page as specified, providing clear frontend development guidance.\n- Data schemas provide field order, types, purpose, and examples for backend data processing.\n\nThis completes the comprehensive design specification for the FoodDelivery web application.\n\n---\n\n",

type=\"button\" id=\"back-to-dashboard\">Back to Dashboard</button></a>\n        </form>\n    </div>\n</body>\n</html>\n\n=== user_task_description ===\n\n# Requirements Document for 'FoodDelivery' Web Application\n\n## 1. Objective\nDevelop a comprehensive web application named 'FoodDelivery' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse restaurants, view menus, place food orders, track deliveries, and write reviews. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.\n\n## 2. Language\nThe required development language for the 'FoodDelivery' application is Python.\n\n## 3. Page Design\n\nThe 'FoodDelivery' web application will consist of the following nine pages:\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Food Delivery Dashboard\n- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured restaurants, popular cuisines, and quick navigation to all functionalities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - **ID: featured-restaurants** - Type: Div - Display of featured restaurant recommendations.\n  - **ID: browse-restaurants-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to restaurant listing page.\n  - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.\n  - **ID: active-orders-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to active orders page.\n\n### 2. Restaurant Listing Page\n- **Page Title**: Browse Restaurants\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available restaurants with search and filter capabilities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: restaurants-page** - Type: Div - Container for the restaurants page.\n  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search restaurants by name or cuisine type.\n  - **ID: cuisine-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by cuisine (Chinese, Italian, Indian, American, etc.).\n  - **ID: restaurants-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying restaurant cards with logo, name, rating, and delivery time.\n  - **ID: view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view restaurant menu (each restaurant card has this).\n\n### 3. Restaurant Menu Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Menu\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed menu items for a specific restaurant with descriptions and prices.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: menu-page** - Type: Div - Container for the menu page.\n  - **ID: restaurant-name** - Type: H1 - Display restaurant name.\n  - **ID: restaurant-info** - Type: Div - Display restaurant info (address, phone, rating).\n  - **ID: menu-items-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying menu items with photos, names, descriptions, and prices.\n  - **ID: add-to-cart-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to add menu item to cart (each item has this).\n  - **ID: view-item-details-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view item details (each menu item has this).\n\n### 4. Item Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Item Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific menu item including ingredients and nutritional info.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: item-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the item details page.\n  - **ID: item-name** - Type: H1 - Display item name.\n  - **ID: item-description** - Type: Div - Display item description and ingredients.\n  - **ID: item-price** - Type: Div - Display item price.\n  - **ID: quantity-input** - Type: Input (number) - Field to select quantity before adding to cart.\n  - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add item with selected quantity to cart.\n\n### 5. Shopping Cart Page\n- **Page Title**: Shopping Cart\n- **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.\n  - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with name, quantity, price, and subtotal.\n  - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).\n  - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).\n  - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.\n  - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.\n\n### 6. Checkout Page\n- **Page Title**: Checkout\n- **Overview**: A page for users to enter delivery information and complete order placement.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.\n  - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.\n  - **ID: delivery-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input delivery address.\n  - **ID: phone-number** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.\n  - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, Cash, PayPal).\n  - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.\n\n### 7. Active Orders Page\n- **Page Title**: Active Orders\n- **Overview**: A page displaying current orders being prepared or delivered with tracking information.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: active-orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the active orders page.\n  - **ID: orders-list** - Type: Div - List displaying active orders with order ID, restaurant, status, and ETA.\n  - **ID: track-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view detailed tracking (each order has this).\n  - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Preparing, On the Way, Delivered).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 8. Order Tracking Page\n- **Page Title**: Track Order\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed order tracking information with delivery person details and real-time status updates.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: tracking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the tracking page.\n  - **ID: order-details** - Type: Div - Display complete order details and timeline.\n  - **ID: delivery-driver-info** - Type: Div - Display delivery driver name, phone, and vehicle info.\n  - **ID: estimated-time** - Type: Div - Display estimated delivery time.\n  - **ID: order-items-list** - Type: Div - List of items in the order.\n  - **ID: back-to-orders** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to active orders.\n\n### 9. Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: Order Reviews\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews for restaurants and allowing users to write new reviews.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with restaurant name, rating, and review text.\n  - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.\n  - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n## 4. Data Storage\n\nThe 'FoodDelivery' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:\n\n### 1. Restaurants Data\n- **File Name**: `restaurants.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00\n  2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00\n  3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00\n  ```\n\n### 2. Menus Data\n- **File Name**: `menus.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1\n  2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1\n  3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1\n  ```\n\n### 3. Cart Data\n- **File Name**: `cart.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|3|2|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n### 4. Orders Data\n- **File Name**: `orders.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234\n  2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678\n  ```\n\n### 5. Order Items Data\n- **File Name**: `order_items.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|12.99\n  2|1|2|1|8.99\n  3|2|3|1|14.99\n  ```\n\n### 6. Deliveries Data\n- **File Name**: `deliveries.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45\n  2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30\n  ```\n\n### 7. Reviews Data\n- **File Name**: `reviews.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12\n  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13\n  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n",

        <label for=\"customer-name-input\">Name:</label>\n            <input type=\"text\" id=\"customer-name-input\" name=\"customer_name\" required /><br />\n            <label type=\"button\" id=\"back-to-dashboard\">Back to Dashboard</button></a>\n        </form>\n    </div>\n</body>\n</html>\n\n=== user_task_description ===\n\n# Requirements Document for 'FoodDelivery' Web Application\n\n## 1. Objective\nDevelop a comprehensive web application named 'FoodDelivery' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse restaurants, view menus, place food orders, track deliveries, and write reviews. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.\n\n## 2. Language\nThe required development language for the 'FoodDelivery' application is Python.\n\n## 3. Page Design\n\nThe 'FoodDelivery' web application will consist of the following nine pages:\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Food Delivery Dashboard\n- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured restaurants, popular cuisines, and quick navigation to all functionalities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - **ID: featured-restaurants** - Type: Div - Display of featured restaurant recommendations.\n  - **ID: browse-restaurants-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to restaurant listing page.\n  - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.\n  - **ID: active-orders-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to active orders page.\n\n### 2. Restaurant Listing Page\n- **Page Title**: Browse Restaurants\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available restaurants with search and filter capabilities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: restaurants-page** - Type: Div - Container for the restaurants page.\n  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search restaurants by name or cuisine type.\n  - **ID: cuisine-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by cuisine (Chinese, Italian, Indian, American, etc.).\n  - **ID: restaurants-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying restaurant cards with logo, name, rating, and delivery time.\n  - **ID: view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view restaurant menu (each restaurant card has this).\n\n### 3. Restaurant Menu Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Menu\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed menu items for a specific restaurant with descriptions and prices.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: menu-page** - Type: Div - Container for the menu page.\n  - **ID: restaurant-name** - Type: H1 - Display restaurant name.\n  - **ID: restaurant-info** - Type: Div - Display restaurant info (address, phone, rating).\n  - **ID: menu-items-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying menu items with photos, names, descriptions, and prices.\n  - **ID: add-to-cart-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to add menu item to cart (each item has this).\n  - **ID: view-item-details-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view item details (each menu item has this).\n\n### 4. Item Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Item Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific menu item including ingredients and nutritional info.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: item-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the item details page.\n  - **ID: item-name** - Type: H1 - Display item name.\n  - **ID: item-description** - Type: Div - Display item description and ingredients.\n  - **ID: item-price** - Type: Div - Display item price.\n  - **ID: quantity-input** - Type: Input (number) - Field to select quantity before adding to cart.\n  - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add item with selected quantity to cart.\n\n### 5. Shopping Cart Page\n- **Page Title**: Shopping Cart\n- **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.\n  - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with name, quantity, price, and subtotal.\n  - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).\n  - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).\n  - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.\n  - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.\n\n### 6. Checkout Page\n- **Page Title**: Checkout\n- **Overview**: A page for users to enter delivery information and complete order placement.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.\n  - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.\n  - **ID: delivery-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input delivery address.\n  - **ID: phone-number** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.\n  - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, Cash, PayPal).\n  - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.\n\n### 7. Active Orders Page\n- **Page Title**: Active Orders\n- **Overview**: A page displaying current orders being prepared or delivered with tracking information.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: active-orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the active orders page.\n  - **ID: orders-list** - Type: Div - List displaying active orders with order ID, restaurant, status, and ETA.\n  - **ID: track-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view detailed tracking (each order has this).\n  - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Preparing, On the Way, Delivered).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 8. Order Tracking Page\n- **Page Title**: Track Order\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed order tracking information with delivery person details and real-time status updates.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: tracking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the tracking page.\n  - **ID: order-details** - Type: Div - Display complete order details and timeline.\n  - **ID: delivery-driver-info** - Type: Div - Display delivery driver name, phone, and vehicle info.\n  - **ID: estimated-time** - Type: Div - Display estimated delivery time.\n  - **ID: order-items-list** - Type: Div - List of items in the order.\n  - **ID: back-to-orders** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to active orders.\n\n### 9. Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: Order Reviews\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews for restaurants and allowing users to write new reviews.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with restaurant name, rating, and review text.\n  - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.\n  - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n## 4. Data Storage\n\nThe 'FoodDelivery' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:\n\n### 1. Restaurants Data\n- **File Name**: `restaurants.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00\n  2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00\n  3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00\n  ```\n\n### 2. Menus Data\n- **File Name**: `menus.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1\n  2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1\n  3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1\n  ```\n\n### 3. Cart Data\n- **File Name**: `cart.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|3|2|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n### 4. Orders Data\n- **File Name**: `orders.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234\n  2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678\n  ```\n\n### 5. Order Items Data\n- **File Name**: `order_items.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|12.99\n  2|1|2|1|8.99\n  3|2|3|1|14.99\n  ```\n\n### 6. Deliveries Data\n- **File Name**: `deliveries.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45\n  2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30\n  ```\n\n### 7. Reviews Data\n- **File Name**: `reviews.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12\n  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13\n  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n",

         | Route Path                     | Function Name             | HTTP Method(s) | Template File         | Context Variables (name: type)                    | Parameters (name: type)           |
         |-------------------------------|---------------------------|----------------|-----------------------|---------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|

         | `/menu/<int:restaurant_id>`  | restaurant_menu           | GET            | menu.html              | restaurant: dict, menu_items: list                 | restaurant_id: int                |
         | `/item/<int:item_id>`         | item_details              | GET            | item_details.html      | item: dict                                      | item_id: int                      |
         | `/cart`                      | view_cart                  | GET            | cart.html              | cart_items: list, total_amount: float              | N/A                              |
         | `/cart/update`               | update_cart                | POST           | N/A                   | N/A                                               | N/A                              |
         | `/checkout`                  | checkout                  | GET, POST      | checkout.html          | (GET) , (POST) order_confirmation: dict or None    | N/A                              |
         | `/orders/active`             | active_orders             | GET            | active_orders.html     | active_orders: list, status_options: list          | N/A                              |
         | `/orders/track/<int:order_id>`| track_order              | GET            | track_order.html       | order: dict, delivery_info: dict, order_items: list | order_id: int                    |
         | `/reviews`                   | reviews                   | GET            | reviews.html           | reviews: list, rating_filter_options: list         | N/A                              |
         | `/reviews/write`             | write_review              | GET, POST      | write_review.html      | (GET) , (POST) submission_status: bool or None     | N/A                              |
         
         **Explanation:**
         - Root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
         - POST routes are for updating cart and submitting reviews.
         - Template context variables use snake_case naming matching the purpose.
         - Parameter names reflect the dynamic parts of the route.
         
         
         ## 2. HTML Template Specifications
         
         ### 2.1. dashboard.html
         - File Path: templates/dashboard.html
         - Page Title: Food Delivery Dashboard
         - Layout Overview: Container div with featured restaurants and navigation buttons leading to main functionalities.
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div)
           - `featured-restaurants` (Div)
           - `browse-restaurants-button` (Button)
           - `view-cart-button` (Button)
           - `active-orders-button` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `browse-restaurants-button`: url_for('browse_restaurants')
           - `view-cart-button`: url_for('view_cart')
           - `active-orders-button`: url_for('active_orders')
         
         ### 2.2. restaurants.html
         - File Path: templates/restaurants.html
         - Page Title: Browse Restaurants
         - Layout Overview: Search and filter controls above a grid of restaurant cards.
         - Element IDs:
           - `restaurants-page` (Div)
           - `search-input` (Input)
           - `cuisine-filter` (Dropdown)
           - `restaurants-grid` (Div)
           - `view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}`: url_for('restaurant_menu', restaurant_id=restaurant_id)
         - Dynamic Element ID Pattern:
           - Buttons in restaurant cards: `view-restaurant-button-{{ restaurant_id }}`
         
         ### 2.3. menu.html
         - File Path: templates/menu.html
         - Page Title: Restaurant Menu
         - Layout Overview: Restaurant info header followed by a grid of menu items.
         - Element IDs:
           - `menu-page` (Div)
           - `restaurant-name` (H1)
           - `restaurant-info` (Div)
           - `menu-items-grid` (Div)
           - `add-to-cart-button-{item_id}` (Button)
           - `view-item-details-{item_id}` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `add-to-cart-button-{item_id}`: (functionality to add item to cart)
           - `view-item-details-{item_id}`: url_for('item_details', item_id=item_id)
         - Dynamic Element ID Pattern:
           - Add to Cart Buttons: `add-to-cart-button-{{ item_id }}`
           - View Details Buttons: `view-item-details-{{ item_id }}`
         
         ### 2.4. item_details.html
         - File Path: templates/item_details.html
         - Page Title: Item Details
         - Layout Overview: Detailed view of a menu item with quantity input and add to cart button.
         - Element IDs:
           - `item-details-page` (Div)
           - `item-name` (H1)
           - `item-description` (Div)
           - `item-price` (Div)
           - `quantity-input` (Input number)
           - `add-to-cart-button` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `add-to-cart-button`: (adds item with quantity to cart)
         
         ### 2.5. cart.html
         - File Path: templates/cart.html
         - Page Title: Shopping Cart
         - Layout Overview: Table of cart items with quantity inputs and remove buttons plus checkout button.
         - Element IDs:
           - `cart-page` (Div)
           - `cart-items-table` (Table)
           - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input number)
           - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button)
           - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button)
           - `total-amount` (Div)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `proceed-checkout-button`: url_for('checkout')
         - Dynamic Element ID Pattern:
           - Quantity Inputs: `update-quantity-{{ item_id }}`
           - Remove Buttons: `remove-item-button-{{ item_id }}`
         
         ### 2.6. checkout.html
         - File Path: templates/checkout.html
         - Page Title: Checkout
         - Layout Overview: Form with fields for delivery and payment info and place order button.
         - Element IDs:
           - `checkout-page` (Div)
           - `customer-name` (Input)
           - `delivery-address` (Textarea)
           - `phone-number` (Input)
           - `payment-method` (Dropdown)
           - `place-order-button` (Button)
         
         ### 2.7. active_orders.html
         - File Path: templates/active_orders.html
         - Page Title: Active Orders
         - Layout Overview: List of current orders with filter and buttons to track orders.
         - Element IDs:
           - `active-orders-page` (Div)
           - `orders-list` (Div)
           - `track-order-button-{order_id}` (Button)
           - `status-filter` (Dropdown)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard')
           - `track-order-button-{order_id}`: url_for('track_order', order_id=order_id)
         - Dynamic Element ID Pattern:
           - Track Buttons: `track-order-button-{{ order_id }}`
         
         ### 2.8. track_order.html
         - File Path: templates/track_order.html
         - Page Title: Track Order
         - Layout Overview: Display detailed tracking info with back button.
         - Element IDs:
           - `tracking-page` (Div)
           - `order-details` (Div)
           - `delivery-driver-info` (Div)
           - `estimated-time` (Div)
           - `order-items-list` (Div)
           - `back-to-orders` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-orders`: url_for('active_orders')
         
         ### 2.9. reviews.html
         - File Path: templates/reviews.html
         - Page Title: Order Reviews
         - Layout Overview: List of reviews with filtering and navigation buttons.
         - Element IDs:
           - `reviews-page` (Div)
           - `reviews-list` (Div)
           - `write-review-button` (Button)
           - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `write-review-button`: url_for('write_review')
           - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard')
         
         ### 2.10. write_review.html
         - File Path: templates/write_review.html
         - Page Title: Write Review
         - Layout Overview: Form to submit a review.
         - Element IDs:
           - `write-review-page` (Div)  <!-- Note: not specified in requirements, logically added -->
           - `review-form` (Form)       <!-- Logical grouping -->
           - `restaurant-select` (Dropdown) <!-- Presumed for selecting a restaurant when writing review -->
           - `customer-name-input` (Input)  <!-- For entering customer name -->
           - `rating-select` (Dropdown)      <!-- For selecting rating -->
           - `review-textarea` (Textarea)    <!-- For review text -->
           - `submit-review-button` (Button) <!-- For submitting review -->
         
         *(Note: The write review page elements and IDs are inferred logically since the requirements specify navigation but not page elements explicitly.)*
         
         ---
         
         ## 3. Data Schemas
         
         ### 3.1. restaurants.txt
         - File name: restaurants.txt
         - Fields (order separated by | ): restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order
         - Purpose: Stores restaurant details including identification, cuisine type, location, contact, rating, delivery time, and minimum order amount.
         - Data types:
           - restaurant_id: int
           - name: string
           - cuisine: string
           - address: string
           - phone: string
           - rating: float
           - delivery_time: int (minutes)
           - min_order: float
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00
           2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00
           3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00
           ```
         
         ### 3.2. menus.txt
         - File name: menus.txt
         - Fields: item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability
         - Purpose: Stores menu items belonging to restaurants, their categorization, descriptions, prices, and availability status.
         - Data types:
           - item_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - item_name: string
           - category: string
           - description: string
           - price: float
           - availability: int (1 or 0)
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1
           2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1
           3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1
           ```
         
         ### 3.3. cart.txt
         - File name: cart.txt
         - Fields: cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date
         - Purpose: Stores the current shopping cart items with quantities and added dates.
         - Data types:
           - cart_id: int
           - item_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - quantity: int
           - added_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|1|1|2|2025-01-15
           2|3|2|1|2025-01-16
           ```
         
         ### 3.4. orders.txt
         - File name: orders.txt
         - Fields: order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number
         - Purpose: Stores order records including customer info, restaurant, order date, amount, status, and delivery info.
         - Data types:
           - order_id: int
           - customer_name: string
           - restaurant_id: int
           - order_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
           - total_amount: float
           - status: string
           - delivery_address: string
           - phone_number: string
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234
           2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678
           ```
         
         ### 3.5. order_items.txt
         - File name: order_items.txt
         - Fields: order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price
         - Purpose: Stores individual items per order, quantities, and price at order time.
         - Data types:
           - order_item_id: int
           - order_id: int
           - item_id: int
           - quantity: int
           - price: float
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|1|1|2|12.99
           2|1|2|1|8.99
           3|2|3|1|14.99
           ```
         
         ### 3.6. deliveries.txt
         - File name: deliveries.txt
         - Fields: delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time
         - Purpose: Stores delivery details including driver information, vehicle, delivery status, and ETA.
         - Data types:
           - delivery_id: int
           - order_id: int
           - driver_name: string
           - driver_phone: string
           - vehicle_info: string
           - status: string
           - estimated_time: date-time string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45
           2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30
           ```
         
         ### 3.7. reviews.txt
         - File name: reviews.txt
         - Fields: review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date
         - Purpose: Stores customer reviews for restaurants including rating and review text.
         - Data types:
           - review_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - customer_name: string
           - rating: int (stars)
           - review_text: string
           - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12
           2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13
           3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15
           ```
         
         ---
         
         ### Notes:
         - The root `/` route redirects to `/dashboard` to comply with start page requirement.
         - The write review page element IDs are inferred as the original description lacks specific IDs and elements for that page.
         - All context and variable names adhere strictly to snake_case.
         - All element IDs use exact casing and spelling as provided.
         - Navigation IDs map exactly to route functions using Flask's `url_for()` in parentheses.
         - Templates reflect each page as specified, providing clear frontend development guidance.
         - Data schemas provide field order, types, purpose, and examples for backend data processing.
         
         This completes the comprehensive design specification for the FoodDelivery web application.

      Type: STRESS_CHAOS_WORD_SHUFFLE

      Before (full content):
         Implement all HTML templates (*.html) based on Section 2 of design_spec.md, ensuring exact layouts, element IDs, page titles, and navigation
         === design_spec.md ===
         # FoodDelivery Web Application Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## 1. Flask Routes Specification
         
         | Route Path                     | Function Name             | HTTP Method(s) | Template File         | Context Variables (name: type)                    | Parameters (name: type)           |
         |-------------------------------|---------------------------|----------------|-----------------------|---------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|
         | `/`                           | root_redirect             | GET            | N/A                   | N/A                                               | N/A                              |
         | `/dashboard`                  | dashboard                 | GET            | dashboard.html         | featured_restaurants: list, popular_cuisines: list | N/A                              |
         | `/restaurants`                | browse_restaurants         | GET            | restaurants.html       | restaurants: list, cuisine_options: list           | N/A                              |
         | `/menu/<int:restaurant_id>`  | restaurant_menu           | GET            | menu.html              | restaurant: dict, menu_items: list                 | restaurant_id: int                |
         | `/item/<int:item_id>`         | item_details              | GET            | item_details.html      | item: dict                                      | item_id: int                      |
         | `/cart`                      | view_cart                  | GET            | cart.html              | cart_items: list, total_amount: float              | N/A                              |
         | `/cart/update`               | update_cart                | POST           | N/A                   | N/A                                               | N/A                              |
         | `/checkout`                  | checkout                  | GET, POST      | checkout.html          | (GET) , (POST) order_confirmation: dict or None    | N/A                              |
         | `/orders/active`             | active_orders             | GET            | active_orders.html     | active_orders: list, status_options: list          | N/A                              |
         | `/orders/track/<int:order_id>`| track_order              | GET            | track_order.html       | order: dict, delivery_info: dict, order_items: list | order_id: int                    |
         | `/reviews`                   | reviews                   | GET            | reviews.html           | reviews: list, rating_filter_options: list         | N/A                              |
         | `/reviews/write`             | write_review              | GET, POST      | write_review.html      | (GET) , (POST) submission_status: bool or None     | N/A                              |
         
         **Explanation:**
         - Root route `/` redirects to `/dashboard`.
         - POST routes are for updating cart and submitting reviews.
         - Template context variables use snake_case naming matching the purpose.
         - Parameter names reflect the dynamic parts of the route.
         
         
         ## 2. HTML Template Specifications
         
         ### 2.1. dashboard.html
         - File Path: templates/dashboard.html
         - Page Title: Food Delivery Dashboard
         - Layout Overview: Container div with featured restaurants and navigation buttons leading to main functionalities.
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div)
           - `featured-restaurants` (Div)
           - `browse-restaurants-button` (Button)
           - `view-cart-button` (Button)
           - `active-orders-button` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `browse-restaurants-button`: url_for('browse_restaurants')
           - `view-cart-button`: url_for('view_cart')
           - `active-orders-button`: url_for('active_orders')
         
         ### 2.2. restaurants.html
         - File Path: templates/restaurants.html
         - Page Title: Browse Restaurants
         - Layout Overview: Search and filter controls above a grid of restaurant cards.
         - Element IDs:
           - `restaurants-page` (Div)
           - `search-input` (Input)
           - `cuisine-filter` (Dropdown)
           - `restaurants-grid` (Div)
           - `view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}`: url_for('restaurant_menu', restaurant_id=restaurant_id)
         - Dynamic Element ID Pattern:
           - Buttons in restaurant cards: `view-restaurant-button-{{ restaurant_id }}`
         
         ### 2.3. menu.html
         - File Path: templates/menu.html
         - Page Title: Restaurant Menu
         - Layout Overview: Restaurant info header followed by a grid of menu items.
         - Element IDs:
           - `menu-page` (Div)
           - `restaurant-name` (H1)
           - `restaurant-info` (Div)
           - `menu-items-grid` (Div)
           - `add-to-cart-button-{item_id}` (Button)
           - `view-item-details-{item_id}` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `add-to-cart-button-{item_id}`: (functionality to add item to cart)
           - `view-item-details-{item_id}`: url_for('item_details', item_id=item_id)
         - Dynamic Element ID Pattern:
           - Add to Cart Buttons: `add-to-cart-button-{{ item_id }}`
           - View Details Buttons: `view-item-details-{{ item_id }}`
         
         ### 2.4. item_details.html
         - File Path: templates/item_details.html
         - Page Title: Item Details
         - Layout Overview: Detailed view of a menu item with quantity input and add to cart button.
         - Element IDs:
           - `item-details-page` (Div)
           - `item-name` (H1)
           - `item-description` (Div)
           - `item-price` (Div)
           - `quantity-input` (Input number)
           - `add-to-cart-button` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `add-to-cart-button`: (adds item with quantity to cart)
         
         ### 2.5. cart.html
         - File Path: templates/cart.html
         - Page Title: Shopping Cart
         - Layout Overview: Table of cart items with quantity inputs and remove buttons plus checkout button.
         - Element IDs:
           - `cart-page` (Div)
           - `cart-items-table` (Table)
           - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (Input number)
           - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (Button)
           - `proceed-checkout-button` (Button)
           - `total-amount` (Div)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `proceed-checkout-button`: url_for('checkout')
         - Dynamic Element ID Pattern:
           - Quantity Inputs: `update-quantity-{{ item_id }}`
           - Remove Buttons: `remove-item-button-{{ item_id }}`
         
         ### 2.6. checkout.html
         - File Path: templates/checkout.html
         - Page Title: Checkout
         - Layout Overview: Form with fields for delivery and payment info and place order button.
         - Element IDs:
           - `checkout-page` (Div)
           - `customer-name` (Input)
           - `delivery-address` (Textarea)
           - `phone-number` (Input)
           - `payment-method` (Dropdown)
           - `place-order-button` (Button)
         
         ### 2.7. active_orders.html
         - File Path: templates/active_orders.html
         - Page Title: Active Orders
         - Layout Overview: List of current orders with filter and buttons to track orders.
         - Element IDs:
           - `active-orders-page` (Div)
           - `orders-list` (Div)
           - `track-order-button-{order_id}` (Button)
           - `status-filter` (Dropdown)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard')
           - `track-order-button-{order_id}`: url_for('track_order', order_id=order_id)
         - Dynamic Element ID Pattern:
           - Track Buttons: `track-order-button-{{ order_id }}`
         
         ### 2.8. track_order.html
         - File Path: templates/track_order.html
         - Page Title: Track Order
         - Layout Overview: Display detailed tracking info with back button.
         - Element IDs:
           - `tracking-page` (Div)
           - `order-details` (Div)
           - `delivery-driver-info` (Div)
           - `estimated-time` (Div)
           - `order-items-list` (Div)
           - `back-to-orders` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-orders`: url_for('active_orders')
         
         ### 2.9. reviews.html
         - File Path: templates/reviews.html
         - Page Title: Order Reviews
         - Layout Overview: List of reviews with filtering and navigation buttons.
         - Element IDs:
           - `reviews-page` (Div)
           - `reviews-list` (Div)
           - `write-review-button` (Button)
           - `filter-by-rating` (Dropdown)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `write-review-button`: url_for('write_review')
           - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for('dashboard')
         
         ### 2.10. write_review.html
         - File Path: templates/write_review.html
         - Page Title: Write Review
         - Layout Overview: Form to submit a review.
         - Element IDs:
           - `write-review-page` (Div)  <!-- Note: not specified in requirements, logically added -->
           - `review-form` (Form)       <!-- Logical grouping -->
           - `restaurant-select` (Dropdown) <!-- Presumed for selecting a restaurant when writing review -->
           - `customer-name-input` (Input)  <!-- For entering customer name -->
           - `rating-select` (Dropdown)      <!-- For selecting rating -->
           - `review-textarea` (Textarea)    <!-- For review text -->
           - `submit-review-button` (Button) <!-- For submitting review -->
         
         *(Note: The write review page elements and IDs are inferred logically since the requirements specify navigation but not page elements explicitly.)*
         
         ---
         
         ## 3. Data Schemas
         
         ### 3.1. restaurants.txt
         - File name: restaurants.txt
         - Fields (order separated by | ): restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order
         - Purpose: Stores restaurant details including identification, cuisine type, location, contact, rating, delivery time, and minimum order amount.
         - Data types:
           - restaurant_id: int
           - name: string
           - cuisine: string
           - address: string
           - phone: string
           - rating: float
           - delivery_time: int (minutes)
           - min_order: float
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00
           2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00
           3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00
           ```
         
         ### 3.2. menus.txt
         - File name: menus.txt
         - Fields: item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability
         - Purpose: Stores menu items belonging to restaurants, their categorization, descriptions, prices, and availability status.
         - Data types:
           - item_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - item_name: string
           - category: string
           - description: string
           - price: float
           - availability: int (1 or 0)
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1
           2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1
           3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1
           ```
         
         ### 3.3. cart.txt
         - File name: cart.txt
         - Fields: cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date
         - Purpose: Stores the current shopping cart items with quantities and added dates.
         - Data types:
           - cart_id: int
           - item_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - quantity: int
           - added_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|1|1|2|2025-01-15
           2|3|2|1|2025-01-16
           ```
         
         ### 3.4. orders.txt
         - File name: orders.txt
         - Fields: order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number
         - Purpose: Stores order records including customer info, restaurant, order date, amount, status, and delivery info.
         - Data types:
           - order_id: int
           - customer_name: string
           - restaurant_id: int
           - order_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
           - total_amount: float
           - status: string
           - delivery_address: string
           - phone_number: string
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234
           2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678
           ```
         
         ### 3.5. order_items.txt
         - File name: order_items.txt
         - Fields: order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price
         - Purpose: Stores individual items per order, quantities, and price at order time.
         - Data types:
           - order_item_id: int
           - order_id: int
           - item_id: int
           - quantity: int
           - price: float
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|1|1|2|12.99
           2|1|2|1|8.99
           3|2|3|1|14.99
           ```
         
         ### 3.6. deliveries.txt
         - File name: deliveries.txt
         - Fields: delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time
         - Purpose: Stores delivery details including driver information, vehicle, delivery status, and ETA.
         - Data types:
           - delivery_id: int
           - order_id: int
           - driver_name: string
           - driver_phone: string
           - vehicle_info: string
           - status: string
           - estimated_time: date-time string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45
           2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30
           ```
         
         ### 3.7. reviews.txt
         - File name: reviews.txt
         - Fields: review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date
         - Purpose: Stores customer reviews for restaurants including rating and review text.
         - Data types:
           - review_id: int
           - restaurant_id: int
           - customer_name: string
           - rating: int (stars)
           - review_text: string
           - review_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Example rows:
           ```
           1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12
           2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13
           3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15
           ```
         
         ---
         
         ### Notes:
         - The root `/` route redirects to `/dashboard` to comply with start page requirement.
         - The write review page element IDs are inferred as the original description lacks specific IDs and elements for that page.
         - All context and variable names adhere strictly to snake_case.
         - All element IDs use exact casing and spelling as provided.
         - Navigation IDs map exactly to route functions using Flask's `url_for()` in parentheses.
         - Templates reflect each page as specified, providing clear frontend development guidance.
         - Data schemas provide field order, types, purpose, and examples for backend data processing.
         
         This completes the comprehensive design specification for the FoodDelivery web application.
         
         ---
